# -*- ck2.landed_titles -*-

# summary of all changes from vanilla landed_titles:
# comment header added.
# lt_allow_annotate.py (title_basic allows).
# shiite -> ismaili except e_shiite, d_shiite, and holy sites
# haruriyyah_composition for haruriyyah
# allow for e_hre
# allows for k_saxon, k_franconia, and k_swabia
# allows for e_roman_empire, k_byzantium, e_byzantium
# k_trebizond color2 and crusade weights
# add k_nikaea
# split k_cilicia from k_anatolia
# syriac holy sites: c_karin, c_mesopotamia, c_alexandria, c_jerusalem, c_antiocheia
# allow for e_persia
# allows for k_aquitaine, e_france
# allows for k_leon, k_spanish_galicia
# e_kanem capital
# d_mzab capital
# c_vaud color and color2
# d_penthievre capital
# d_mudar capital
# c_tui color2
# d_sibir capital
# d_yaroslavl capital
# d_livonia capital
# d_samogitia capital
# d_tioharad capital
# d_corsica color
# d_abkhazia capital
# allow for e_seljuk_turks
# allow for e_india
# added d_livonian_brothers_of_the_sword from SWMH
# removed allow triggers from titular titles without capitals, as per vanilla

# SPECIAL TITLES
e_outremer = {
	color = { 180 180 180 }
	color2 = { 255 255 255 }
	capital = 774 # Jerusalem
	allow = {
		conditional_tooltip = {
			trigger = {
				NAND = {
					is_heretic = no
					OR = {
						religion = catholic
						religion = cathar
						religion = fraticelli
						religion = waldensian
						religion = lollard
						religion = adoptionist
						religion = arian
					}
				}
			}
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = catholic
				religion = cathar
				religion = fraticelli
				religion = waldensian
				religion = lollard
				religion = adoptionist
				religion = arian
			}
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_de_jure_title = no } }
			FROM = { is_de_jure_title = yes }
		}
		title_emperor_basic_allow = yes
	}
} # end e_outremer

k_papal_state = {
	color = { 255 249 198 }
	color2 = { 220 220 0 }
	capital = 333 # Rome
	title = POPE
	foa = POPE_FOA
	short_name = yes
	location_ruler_title = yes
	# Always exists
	landless = yes
	# Controls a religion
	controls_religion = catholic
	religion = catholic
	# Cannot be held as a secondary title
	primary = yes
	
	assimilate = no
	
	dynasty_title_names = no # Will not be named "Seljuk", etc.
	
	dignity = 200
	
	# Regnal names
	male_names = {
		Alexander Anastasius Benedictus Caelestinus Callistus Clemens Eugenius Leo Gregorius Hadrianus Honorius Innocentius
		Ioannes Lucius Marinus Martinus Nicolaus Sergius Silvester Stephanus Urbanus Victor
	}
}

d_sunni = {
	color = { 40 160 40 }
	color2 = { 220 220 0 }
	capital = 719 # Mecca
	creation_requires_capital = no
	dignity = 100 # Counted as having this many more counties than it does
	title = CALIPH
	title_female = CALIPHA
	foa = CALIPH_FOA
	short_name = yes
	religion = sunni
	# Controls a religion
	controls_religion = sunni
	caliphate = yes
	coat_of_arms = {
		data = { 0 0 0 3 0 2 2 }
		religion = sunni
	}
	allow = {
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { religion = sunni } }
			religion = sunni
		}
		OR = {
			trait = mirza
			trait = sayyid
			piety = 1000
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } } }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = sunni_creation_independent
				in_revolt = no
				OR = {
					independent = yes
					NOT = {
						any_liege = {
							OR = {
								in_revolt = yes
								NOT = { religion = sunni }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = sayyid
					piety = 1000
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = destroyed_caliphates } }
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = controls_mecca_medina
						c_mecca = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
						c_medina = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = controls_jerusalem_damascus_baghdad
					c_jerusalem = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
					c_damascus = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
					c_baghdad = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_else = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = THREE_HOLY_SITES_TT
				any_realm_title = {
					count = 3
					is_holy_site = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = destroyed_caliphates }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = controls_mecca_medina
				c_mecca = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
				c_medina = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
	}
}

e_hre = { # Created by special decision, mostly
	color = { 250 250 250 }
	color2 = { 0 0 0 }
	capital = 90 # Jülich / Aachen
	short_name = yes
	allow = {
		FROM = {
			has_holder = yes
			is_de_jure_title = yes
		}
		OR = {
			realm_size = 220
			AND = {
				realm_size = 120
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = { has_holder = no }
						primary_title = {
							OR = {
								has_law = crown_authority_3
								has_law = crown_authority_4
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						has_holder = yes
						has_law = crown_authority_4
					}
				}
			}
		}
		title_emperor_basic_allow = yes
	}
	
	k_saxon = {
		color={ 70 70 70 }
		color2={ 255 255 255 }

		capital = 257

		title_prefix = "GRAND_DUCHY_PREFIX"
		title = "GRAND_DUCHY_RULER"
		title_female = "GRAND_DUCHY_RULER_FEMALE"

		allow = {
			conditional_tooltip = {
				trigger = {
					k_saxon = {
						is_de_jure_title = no
					}
				}
				k_saxon = {
					is_de_jure_title = yes
				}
			}
			title_king_basic_allow = yes
		}

		catholic = 3000 # Crusade target weight
		norse_pagan_reformed = 500 # Crusade target weight
	}

d_ibadi = {
	color = { 20 130 20 }
	color2 = { 220 220 0 }
	capital = 719 # Mecca
	creation_requires_capital = no
	dignity = 80 # Counted as having this many more counties than it does
	title = CALIPH
	title_female = CALIPHA
	foa = CALIPH_FOA
	short_name = yes
	religion = ibadi
	# Controls a religion
	controls_religion = ibadi
	caliphate = yes
	coat_of_arms = {
		data = { 0 0 0 8 0 2 2 }
		religion = ibadi
	}
	allow = {
		OR = {
			trait = mirza
			trait = sayyid
			piety = 1000
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } } }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = ibadi_creation_independent
				hidden_tooltip = {
					in_revolt = no
					OR = {
						independent = yes
						NOT = {
							any_liege = {
								OR = {
									in_revolt = yes
									NOT = { religion = ibadi }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = sayyid
					piety = 1000
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = destroyed_caliphates } }
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = controls_mecca_medina
						hidden_tooltip = {
							c_mecca = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
							c_medina = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = controls_jerusalem_damascus_baghdad
					hidden_tooltip = {
						c_jerusalem = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
						c_damascus = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
						c_baghdad = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_else = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = THREE_HOLY_SITES_TT
				hidden_tooltip = {
					any_realm_title = {
						count = 3
						is_holy_site = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = destroyed_caliphates }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = controls_mecca_medina
				hidden_tooltip = {
					c_mecca = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
					c_medina = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
